 An MLA can ask 40 starred and over 60 unstarred questions in a budget session
 yani ek vidhayak ek bajet satr main 100 prashn puch saktaa he
 In a normal session, one can ask 10 starred and 20 unstarred questions
 prashn ke liye kam se kam 14 din pehle sachiv ko soochna deni hoti he
 Answers to the starred question are given orally in the House
 atarankit prashn ke jawaab sadsy ko likhit rup se die jate hai
 If a question is not answered on a given day, the answer to this question is published in writing in the proceedings of that day

 But when it came to the BJP leader, the police is now making an excuse that we are investigating the allegations
